                "Id" uuid NOT NULL DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),

            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "tenant_demo"."Users" (
                "Id" uuid NOT NULL,

            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "tenant_demo"."UserProfiles" (

            ALTER TABLE IF EXISTS "tenant_demo"."Sessions" ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS "Transcript" text NULL;
            ALTER TABLE IF EXISTS "tenant_demo"."Sessions" ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS "PassScore" int NOT NULL DEFAULT 70;
            ALTER TABLE IF EXISTS "tenant_demo"."Sessions" ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS "DurationMinutes" int NOT NULL DEFAULT 0;

            -- Migrate existing Lessons rows → Sessions (idempotent via ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING)
            INSERT INTO "tenant_demo"."Sessions"
                ("Id", "ModuleId", "Title", "Description", "OrderIndex", "IsFreeTrial",
                 "PublishStatus", "SessionType", "Content", "AudioUrl", "DocumentUrl",
                 "Transcript", "PassScore", "DurationMinutes", "ThumbnailUrl", "CreatedAt")
            SELECT
                l."Id", l."ModuleId", l."Title", l."Description", l."OrderIndex", l."IsFreeTrial",
                l."PublishStatus",
                CASE l."LessonType"
                    WHEN 'Reading' THEN 'Reading'
                    WHEN 'Audio'   THEN 'Audio'
                    WHEN 'Pdf'     THEN 'Pdf'
                    WHEN 'Quiz'    THEN 'Quiz'
                    ELSE 'Video'
                END,
                l."Content", l."AudioUrl", l."DocumentUrl",
                l."Transcript", l."PassScore", l."DurationMinutes", l."ThumbnailUrl", l."CreatedAt"
            FROM "tenant_demo"."Lessons" l
            WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.tables WHERE table_schema = 'tenant_demo' AND table_name = 'Lessons')
            ON CONFLICT ("Id") DO NOTHING;

            -- Create default Segment for each migrated Lesson that has none yet
            INSERT INTO "tenant_demo"."Segments"
                ("Id", "SessionId", "Title", "StartTime", "EndTime", "OrderIndex", "CreatedAt")
            SELECT gen_random_uuid(), l."Id", 'Nội dung chính', 0, 0, 0, now()
            FROM "tenant_demo"."Lessons" l
            WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.tables WHERE table_schema = 'tenant_demo' AND table_name = 'Lessons')
              AND EXISTS  (SELECT 1 FROM "tenant_demo"."Sessions" s WHERE s."Id" = l."Id")
              AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM "tenant_demo"."Segments" seg WHERE seg."SessionId" = l."Id");

[14:21:02 INF] Executed DbCommand (2ms) [Parameters=[@ids='?' (DbType = Object)], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']

FROM (
    SELECT s."ConversationId"
    FROM "SupportMessages" AS s
    WHERE s."ConversationId" = ANY (@ids)
    GROUP BY s."ConversationId"
) AS s1
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT s2."Id", s2."Content", s2."ConversationId", s2."CreatedAt", s2."FileName", s2."FileUrl", s2."MimeType", s2."SenderId", s2."SenderRole", s2."SizeBytes", s2."Type", s2."UpdatedAt"
    FROM (
        SELECT s0."Id", s0."Content", s0."ConversationId", s0."CreatedAt", s0."FileName", s0."FileUrl", s0."MimeType", s0."SenderId", s0."SenderRole", s0."SizeBytes", s0."Type", s0."UpdatedAt", ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY s0."ConversationId" ORDER BY s0."CreatedAt" DESC) AS row
        FROM "SupportMessages" AS s0
        WHERE s0."ConversationId" = ANY (@ids)
    ) AS s2
    WHERE s2.row <= 1
) AS s3 ON s1."ConversationId" = s3."ConversationId"
